padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: x-small; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;第三、四项&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;/td&gt;\n&lt;/tr&gt;\n&lt;tr style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;\n&lt;td style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px 7px; word-break: break-all; max-width: 100%; word-wrap: break-word !important; box-sizing: border-box !important; border: 1px none none solid #dddddd #dddddd black;&quot; width=&quot;177&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: x-small; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;&quot;&gt;&lt;strong style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;海淘代购&lt;/span&gt;/&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;境外购物消费&lt;/span&gt; &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;/td&gt;\n&lt;td style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px 7px; word-break: break-all; max-width: 100%; word-wrap: break-word !important; box-sizing: border-box !important; border: 1px none none solid #dddddd #dddddd black;&quot; width=&quot;180&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: x-small; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;无&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;/td&gt;\n&lt;td style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px 7px; word-break: break-all; max-width: 100%; word-wrap: break-word !important; box-sizing: border-box !important; border: 1px none none solid #dddddd #dddddd black;&quot; width=&quot;100&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: x-small; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;第四项&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;/td&gt;\n&lt;/tr&gt;\n&lt;/tbody&gt;\n&lt;/table&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #3e3e3e; font-family: \'Helvetica Neue\', Helvetica, \'Hiragino Sans GB\', \'Microsoft YaHei\', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: x-small; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;（注意：此处我们严格区分跨境电商和海淘代购，其根本区别在于是否经过海关备案并按要求进行三单比对）&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #3e3e3e; font-family: \'Helvetica Neue\', Helvetica, \'Hiragino Sans GB\', \'Microsoft YaHei\', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;br style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot; /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #3e3e3e; font-family: \'Helvetica Neue\', Helvetica, \'Hiragino Sans GB\', \'Microsoft YaHei\', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-size: x-small;&quot;&gt;当然了，以上解读过于直白，似乎国家在政策制定方面&amp;ldquo;功利性&amp;rdquo;很强，一心只为自身经济增长。实际上，我们可以用另一条逻辑来解读以上会议决议：首先，扩大进口，有助于我国进出口贸易的平衡，营造一个公平的国际贸易环境。我国过去的强劲出口已经招来不少贸易摩擦，如果我国主动扩大进口，将有助于在我国与他国的双边或多边贸易谈判，进而改善我国的出口环境。第二，扩大进口，能为中国人提供更丰富的消费选择，进而提高人民生活质量。第三，扩大进口，有助于倒逼中国消费品制造业的转型，促使他们在更加激烈的市场环境中寻求发展之道。&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #3e3e3e; font-family: \'Helvetica Neue\', Helvetica, \'Hiragino Sans GB\', \'Microsoft YaHei\', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #3e3e3e; font-family: \'Helvetica Neue\', Helvetica, \'Hiragino Sans GB\', \'Microsoft YaHei\', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: x-small;&quot;&gt;&lt;strong style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: #00b050; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;国务院决议对进口跨境电商的影响&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #3e3e3e; font-family: \'Helvetica Neue\', Helvetica, \'Hiragino Sans GB\', \'Microsoft YaHei\', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #3e3e3e; font-family: \'Helvetica Neue\', Helvetica, \'Hiragino Sans GB\', \'Microsoft YaHei\', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-size: x-small;&quot;&gt;从以上分析可以看出，国务院的决议并非主要针对跨境电商。然而，这些决议和跨境电商息息相关。&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #3e3e3e; font-family: \'Helvetica Neue\', Helvetica, \'Hiragino Sans GB\', \'Microsoft YaHei\', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-size: x-small;&quot;&gt;&lt;br style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot; /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #3e3e3e; font-family: \'Helvetica Neue\', Helvetica, \'Hiragino Sans GB\', \'Microsoft YaHei\', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: x-small;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;首先，决议第一项和第二项都是一般贸易进口的利好消息，这可能减少跨境电商的进口量。我们举例说明，某款高端指甲化妆品，按照目前的一般贸易进口方式，关税为&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;15%&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;，增值税&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;17%&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;，消费税&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;30%&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;；如果按照跨境电商进口，仅有行邮税&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;50%&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;。在这种情况下，显然跨境电商进口有优势。按照决议第一项和第二项，国家将关税和消费税调低，那么一般贸易进口该高端化妆品的税额可能要低于跨境电商进口，这样就有可能减少跨境电商进口量。注意，仅仅是存在这种可能性。毕竟，这里还涉及其它两个因素：（&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;）一般贸易进口和跨境电商进口的操作成本不同。对于化妆品，如果要一般贸易进口，则需要先进行前置审批等繁琐流程，采用跨境电商的话，流程就简单多了。（&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;2&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;）跨境电商的税率也可能进行改革。当前跨境电商按照行邮税实行，但业内有传闻，国家正在考虑将采取关税和增值税的方式，并取消免税额度。因此，在当前政策还没有落地之前，我们无法断定这些决议对跨境电商的最终影响。&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #3e3e3e; font-family: \'Helvetica Neue\', Helvetica, \'Hiragino Sans GB\', \'Microsoft YaHei\', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #3e3e3e; font-family: \'Helvetica Neue\', Helvetica, \'Hiragino Sans GB\', \'Microsoft YaHei\', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: x-small;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;其次，决议第四项要求&lt;/span&gt; &lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&amp;ldquo;严格落实进境物品依法主动申报纳税&amp;rdquo;，有利于跨境电商发展。跨境电商是一种阳光化的进口通道，而很多海淘代购则通过邮件&lt;/span&gt;/&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;快件或者人力携带等&amp;ldquo;灰色通道&amp;rdquo;入境。如果国家按照决议第四项严格查处这些灰色通道，将有更多的商品使用跨境电商通道入境，进而促进跨境电商发展。&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #3e3e3e; font-family: \'Helvetica Neue\', Helvetica, \'Hiragino Sans GB\', \'Microsoft YaHei\', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;br style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot; /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #3e3e3e; font-family: \'Helvetica Neue\', Helvetica, \'Hiragino Sans GB\', \'Microsoft YaHei\', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: x-small;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;最后，整体政策导向越来越有助于进口跨境电商的发展。我们对&lt;/span&gt;2012&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;年至&lt;/span&gt;2014&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;年的跨境电商政策进行了梳理，发现：（&lt;/span&gt;1&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;）国务院办公厅颁布了&lt;/span&gt;3&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;份与出口跨境电商相关的文件，&lt;/span&gt;0&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;份涉及进口跨境电商的文件；（&lt;/span&gt;2&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;）质检总局于&lt;/span&gt;2013&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;年&lt;/span&gt;11&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;月出台了《关于支持跨境电子商务零售出口的指导意见》，财政部&lt;/span&gt;/&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;税务总局于&lt;/span&gt;2013&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;年&lt;/span&gt;12&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;月联合出台了《关于跨境电子商务零售出口税收政策的通知》，但截至目前，二者都未出台针对进口跨境电商的政策文件；（&lt;/span&gt;3&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;）仅有海关总署和外管局在发布的跨境电商政策中，将出口跨境电商和进口跨境电商并行。也即，过去几年进口跨境电商在过去并没有得到与出口跨境电商应有的重视。然而，近期我们观察到，进口跨境电商在慢慢得到国家重视：去年&lt;/span&gt;9&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;月，李克强主持的国务院常务会议，确定了加强进口的&lt;/span&gt;5&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;条政策措施，其中包括&amp;ldquo;搭建进口贸易平台，在公平竞争原则下，利用跨境电子商务等新模式增加进口&amp;rdquo;；这一次国务院常务会议中，第四项决议明确要求&amp;ldquo;制定支持跨境电商进口的检验检疫政策&amp;rdquo;，也即质检总局很快会出台针对进口跨境电商的政策文件。从业内传闻得知，财政部&lt;/span&gt;/&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;税务总局也在抓紧制定针对进口跨境电商的税收政策。因此，我们可以明显感受到，整体政策将越来越有利于进口跨境电商的规范发展。&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-size: medium;&quot;&gt;&lt;strong style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;仓储模式:&lt;/strong&gt;亚马逊提供仓储和邮寄服务，就是大家熟知的FBA。或者由卖家自己负责仓储和邮寄。而EBay并不提供EBay官方的仓储。FBA的优势是很明显的，不仅让卖家在亚马逊PRIME用户的曝光率更高，而且在一定程度上省去了卖家仓储，包装和邮寄的麻烦。  现在亚马逊上不少卖家已经使用了FBA, 或者正在考虑FBA。我在使用FBA的同时仍然保留了我长期自建的仓储，一方面是EBay账户的需求，另一方是方便Amazon账户的操作和对于Amazon的差评处理的灵活性。&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #3e3e3e; font-family: \'Helvetica Neue\', Helvetica, \'Hiragino Sans GB\', \'Microsoft YaHei\', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: medium; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #3e3e3e; font-family: \'Helvetica Neue\', Helvetica, \'Hiragino Sans GB\', \'Microsoft YaHei\', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 25px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-size: medium;&quot;&gt;&lt;strong style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;客户群体:&lt;/strong&gt;长期以来，主导型的观点认为亚马逊的用户比ebay的更为&amp;ldquo;优质&amp;rdquo;一些。但是我个人认为，亚马逊的客户反而更难应对一些。尤其是PRIME的会员。用过FBA的卖家都会有同样的经历，或许因为PRIME会有每年要支付一笔会员费，他们对购物过程以及产品都非常挑剔，更容易退货并给卖家差评。据亚马逊的统计，大概只有10%的PRIME会员会主动地留好评。&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; color: #3e3e3e; font-family: \'Helvetica Neue\', Helvetica, \'Hiragino Sans GB\', \'Microsoft YaHei\', Arial, sans-serif; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;&quot;&gt;非常大。对于一个亚马逊的卖家，中评都必须及时处理。原因非常简单，一方面买家评分直接影响销售，另一方面就是影响并决定店铺在亚马逊内部的评级。  当你的评分低于一个等级，就是好评率小与95%，亚马逊会发出官方警告，如果在收到警告后卖家没有及时处理中评和差评，亚马逊会直接关掉评分过低的店铺，甚至把卖家的相关信息录入内部黑名单，卖家以后几乎不可能在亚马逊上开店。对于刚入行的卖家来说，需要简单的记住最基本的三条原则：避免中差评，不违规，及时回答客户问题。&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px; font-size: medium;&quot;&gt;这里也是我为什么仍然在用我的自建仓储做亚马逊的原因。首先自建仓储发出的货品，卖家可以主动的一键退款并告知买家。如果是FBA的货品，则需要买家去向亚马逊申请退款。  其次我的自建仓储可以告知买家他保留现在已经收到的货品，无需退回给我。而FBA则一定要求买家把货退回。当然我的仓储还可以给买家邮寄补偿性的礼物。  从买家体验和卖家的处理态度上来讲，我用自建仓储发出的货品，更容易博得买家的好感，从而为我成功让买家撤掉差评打下基础，90%左右的买家会接受并且愿意去掉差评。这种能力在账户差评率处在危险边缘的时候上显得尤为重要。&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p style=&quot;margin: 0px;
